				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://comfortfoodlite.com/baked-crunchy-hot-honey-chicken/" rel="bookmark">Baked Crunchy Hot Honey Chicken</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-26T17:21:20+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">February 26, 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://comfortfoodlite.com/author/sarah/" title="View all posts by Sarah Johnson" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Sarah Johnson</span></a></span></span> 		</div>
					</header>
			
			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"><p>A simple idea&#x2014;crispy baked chicken finished with a sticky, spicy-sweet honey&#x2014;turns weeknight cooking into a small celebration. This recipe is quick, forgiving, and made with pantry staples. It delivers crunchy &#8230; </p>
<p class="read-more-container"><a title="Baked Crunchy Hot Honey Chicken" class="read-more button" href="https://comfortfoodlite.com/baked-crunchy-hot-honey-chicken/#more-14497" aria-label="Read more about Baked Crunchy Hot Honey Chicken">Learn more</a></p>
